	//写cookie后跳转
	function writeFeeCookie(provincename,citycode){
		var Days = 365;
		var exp = new Date();
		exp.setTime(exp.getTime() + Days*24*60*60*1000);
		// 测试用cookie
		// document.cookie = "CmProvid="+getProvBrief(provincename)+";path=/;expires=" + exp.toGMTString();
		// document.cookie = "CmCitycode="+citycode+";path=/;expires=" + exp.toGMTString();
		// 上线用cookie
		document.cookie = "CmProvid="+getProvBrief(provincename)+";path=/;domain=10086.cn;expires=" + exp.toGMTString();
		document.cookie = "CmCitycode="+citycode+";path=/;domain=10086.cn;expires=" + exp.toGMTString();
		location.href = "fee_list_"+citycode+".html";
	}
	//非省会地市初始化cookie
	
	
		var Days = 365;
		var exp = new Date();
		exp.setTime(exp.getTime() + Days*24*60*60*1000);
		// 测试用cookie
		// document.cookie = "CmProvid="+getProvBrief('黑龙江')+";path=/;expires=" + exp.toGMTString();
		// document.cookie = "CmCitycode=1000451;path=/;expires=" + exp.toGMTString();
		// 上线用cookie
		document.cookie = "CmProvid="+getProvBrief('黑龙江')+";path=/;domain=10086.cn;expires=" + exp.toGMTString();
		document.cookie = "CmCitycode=1000451;path=/;domain=10086.cn;expires=" + exp.toGMTString();

</script>

	//点击排序高亮
	function checkOrderStatus(brand,type,click_order){
	    if($("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_name_order").attr("current")==1){
	        click_order="name";
	    }else{
	        click_order="price";
	    }
	    
	    
		if(click_order=="price"){
			if($("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_name_order").val()=="desc"){
				$("#orderByName").removeClass().addClass("txt_4")
			}else{
				$("#orderByName").removeClass().addClass("txt_5")
			}
			if($("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_order").val()=="desc"){
				$("#orderByPrice").removeClass().addClass("txt_2_c")
			}else{
				$("#orderByPrice").removeClass().addClass("txt_3_c")
			}
		}else{
			if($("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_order").val()=="desc"){
				$("#orderByPrice").removeClass().addClass("txt_2")
			}else{
				$("#orderByPrice").removeClass().addClass("txt_3")
			}
			if($("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_name_order").val()=="desc"){
				$("#orderByName").removeClass().addClass("txt_4_c")
			}else{
				$("#orderByName").removeClass().addClass("txt_5_c")
			}
		}
	}
	
	//排序方法
	function sortMethod(arr,func) {
   // 交换两个数组项的位置
    var swap = function(firstIndex, secondIndex) {
        var temp = arr[firstIndex];
        arr[firstIndex] = arr[secondIndex];
        arr[secondIndex] = temp;
    };
   
    // 升序排列
    var bubbleSort = function() {
         var i, j, stop, len = arr.length;
         for (i=0; i<len; i=i+1) {
             for (j=0, stop = len - i-1; j<stop; j=j+1) {
                  // 将这里的'>'换成'<'即为降序排列
                  if (func(arr[j],arr[j+1])==1) { swap(j, j+1); }
             }
        }
    }();
    }
	
	//按首字排序
	
	function doNameOrder(brand,type){
	
	var ascSpread = function(a,b){
	    if(parseFloat($(a).attr("spread"))==0){
			return 1;
		}else{
			return -1;
		}
	}
	
	var ascApart= function(a,b){
	    if(parseFloat($(a).attr("spread"))==1 && parseFloat($(b).attr("spread"))==0){		
			return -1;
	    }
	
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("packtype"))==2){
			return -1;
		}else{
			return 1;
		}
	}
	
	var descApart= function(a,b){
	    if(parseFloat($(a).attr("spread"))==1 && parseFloat($(b).attr("spread"))==0){		
			return -1;
	    }
	
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("packtype"))==2){
			return 1;
		}else{
			return -1;
		}
	}
	
	var asc = function(a, b) {
        if(parseFloat($(a).attr("spread"))==1 && parseFloat($(b).attr("spread"))==0){		
			return -1;
	    }
		
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("packtype"))==2 && parseFloat($(b).attr("packtype"))==1){		
			return -1;
	    }
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("name")) == parseFloat($(b).attr("name"))){
			if(parseFloat($(a).attr("id")) == parseFloat($(b).attr("id"))){
					return parseFloat($(a).attr("storeid")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("storeid")) ? 1 : -1;
			}else{
			        return parseFloat($(a).attr("id")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("id")) ? 1 : -1;	
            }					
		}else{
			return parseFloat($(a).attr("name")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("name")) ? 1 : -1;
		}
		
	}

	var desc = function(a, b) {
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("spread"))==1 && parseFloat($(b).attr("spread"))==0){		
			return -1;
	    }
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("packtype"))==1 && parseFloat($(b).attr("packtype"))==2){
	    	return -1;
	    }
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("name")) == parseFloat($(b).attr("name"))){
			if(parseFloat($(a).attr("id")) == parseFloat($(b).attr("id"))){
					return parseFloat($(a).attr("storeid")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("storeid")) ? 1 : -1;
			}else{
			        return parseFloat($(a).attr("id")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("id")) ? -1 : 1;
			}
		}else{
			return parseFloat($(a).attr("name")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("name")) ? 1 : -1;
		}
		
	}
	
		if($("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_name_order").val()=="desc"){
			var sortEle_list = $("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_list_default_hidden .feeItem_list").sort(ascSpread);
			var sortEle_big = $("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_big_default_hidden .feeItem_big").sort(ascSpread);
			sortMethod(sortEle_list,descApart);
			sortMethod(sortEle_big,descApart);
			sortMethod(sortEle_list,desc);
			sortMethod(sortEle_big,desc);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_list_default_hidden").empty().append(sortEle_list);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_big_default_hidden").empty().append(sortEle_big);
			$("#orderByName").removeClass().addClass("txt_5");
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_name_order").val("asc");
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_name_order").attr("current",1);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_order").attr("current",0);
		}else{
			var sortEle_list = $("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_list_default_hidden .feeItem_list").sort(ascSpread);
			var sortEle_big = $("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_big_default_hidden .feeItem_big").sort(ascSpread);
			sortMethod(sortEle_list,ascApart);
			sortMethod(sortEle_big,ascApart);
			sortMethod(sortEle_list,asc);
			sortMethod(sortEle_big,asc);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_list_default_hidden").empty().append(sortEle_list);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_big_default_hidden").empty().append(sortEle_big);
			$("#orderByName").removeClass().addClass("txt_4");
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_name_order").val("desc");
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_name_order").attr("current",1);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_order").attr("current",0);
		}	
	}
	
	//排序
	
	function doOrder(brand,type){
		var ascSpread = function(a,b){
	    if(parseFloat($(a).attr("spread"))==0){
			return 1;
		}else{
			return -1;
		}
	    }
		
		
		var asc = function(a, b) {
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("spread"))==1 && parseFloat($(b).attr("spread"))==0){		
			return -1;
	    }
			if(parseFloat($(a).attr("id")) == parseFloat($(b).attr("id"))){
				return parseFloat($(a).attr("storeId")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("storeId")) ? 1 : -1;
			}else{
				return parseFloat($(a).attr("id")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("id")) ? 1 : -1;
			}
		}

		var desc = function(a, b) {
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("spread"))==1 && parseFloat($(b).attr("spread"))==0){		
			return -1;
	    }
			if(parseFloat($(a).attr("id")) == parseFloat($(b).attr("id"))){
					return parseFloat($(a).attr("storeid")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("storeid")) ? 1 : -1;
			}else{
				return parseFloat($(a).attr("id")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("id")) ? -1 : 1;
			}
		}
	
		if($("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_order").val()=="desc"){
			var sortEle_list = $("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_list_default_hidden .feeItem_list").sort(ascSpread);
			var sortEle_big = $("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_big_default_hidden .feeItem_big").sort(ascSpread);		
			sortMethod(sortEle_list,desc);
			sortMethod(sortEle_big,desc);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_list_default_hidden").empty().append(sortEle_list);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_big_default_hidden").empty().append(sortEle_big);
			$("#orderByPrice").removeClass().addClass("txt_3");
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_order").val("asc");
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_order").attr("current",1);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_name_order").attr("current",0);
		}else{
			var sortEle_list = $("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_list_default_hidden .feeItem_list").sort(ascSpread);
			var sortEle_big = $("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_big_default_hidden .feeItem_big").sort(ascSpread);
			sortMethod(sortEle_list,asc);
			sortMethod(sortEle_big,asc);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_list_default_hidden").empty().append(sortEle_list);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_big_default_hidden").empty().append(sortEle_big);
			$("#orderByPrice").removeClass().addClass("txt_2");
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_order").val("desc");
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_order").attr("current",1);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_name_order").attr("current",0);
		}	
	}
	
	function autoOrder(brand,type,order){
	
	var ascSpread = function(a,b){
	    if(parseFloat($(a).attr("spread"))==0){
			return 1;
		}else{
			return -1;
		}
	    }
	
	var ascApart= function(a,b){
	if(parseFloat($(a).attr("spread"))==1 && parseFloat($(b).attr("spread"))==0){		
			return -1;
	    }
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("packType"))==2){
			return -1;
		}else{
			return 1;
		}
	}
	
	var descApart= function(a,b){
	if(parseFloat($(a).attr("spread"))==1 && parseFloat($(b).attr("spread"))==0){		
			return -1;
	    }
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("packType"))==2){
			return 1;
		}else{
			return -1;
		}
	}
	
	var asc = function(a, b) {
        if(parseFloat($(a).attr("spread"))==1 && parseFloat($(b).attr("spread"))==0){		
			return -1;
	    }
		
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("packtype"))==2 && parseFloat($(b).attr("packtype"))==1){		
			return -1;
	    }
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("name")) == parseFloat($(b).attr("name"))){
			if(parseFloat($(a).attr("id")) == parseFloat($(b).attr("id"))){
					return parseFloat($(a).attr("storeid")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("storeid")) ? 1 : -1;
			}else{
			        return parseFloat($(a).attr("id")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("id")) ? 1 : -1;	
            }					
		}else{
			return parseFloat($(a).attr("name")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("name")) ? 1 : -1;
		}
		
	}

	var desc = function(a, b) {
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("spread"))==1 && parseFloat($(b).attr("spread"))==0){		
			return -1;
	    }
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("packtype"))==1 && parseFloat($(b).attr("packtype"))==2){
	    	return -1;
	    }
		if(parseFloat($(a).attr("name")) == parseFloat($(b).attr("name"))){
			if(parseFloat($(a).attr("id")) == parseFloat($(b).attr("id"))){
					return parseFloat($(a).attr("storeid")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("storeid")) ? 1 : -1;
			}else{
			        return parseFloat($(a).attr("id")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("id")) ? -1 : 1;
			}
		}else{
			return parseFloat($(a).attr("name")) > parseFloat($(b).attr("name")) ? 1 : -1;
		}
		
	}
		if(order=="asc"){
			var sortEle_list = $("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_list_default_hidden .feeItem_list").sort(ascSpread);
			var sortEle_big = $("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_big_default_hidden .feeItem_big").sort(ascSpread);
			sortMethod(sortEle_list,ascApart);
			sortMethod(sortEle_big,ascApart);
			sortMethod(sortEle_list,asc);
			sortMethod(sortEle_big,asc);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_list_default_hidden").empty().append(sortEle_list);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_big_default_hidden").empty().append(sortEle_big);
			$("#orderByName").removeClass().addClass("txt_4_c");
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_order").val("desc");
		}else{
			var sortEle_list = $("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_list_default_hidden .feeItem_list").sort(ascSpread);
			var sortEle_big = $("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_big_default_hidden .feeItem_big").sort(ascSpread);			
			sortMethod(sortEle_list,descApart);
			sortMethod(sortEle_big,descApart);
			sortEle_list.sort(desc);
			sortEle_big.sort(desc);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_list_default_hidden").empty().append(sortEle_list);
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_big_default_hidden").empty().append(sortEle_big);
			$("#orderByPrice").removeClass().addClass("txt_5");
			$("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_order").val("asc");
		}	
	}
	
	//获取搜索跳转
	function subform(){		
		var brand="";
		var monUse="";
		var busiTrend="";
		$("#brand input[name = brand]:checkbox").each(
			function(){if($(this).is(':checked')){
			    brand+="-"+$(this).val();
			}}
		)
		$("#busiTrend input[name = busiTrend]:checkbox").each(
			function(){if($(this).is(':checked')){
				busiTrend+="-"+$(this).val();
			}}
		)
		$("#monUse input[name = monUse]:checkbox").each(
			function(){if($(this).is(':checked')){
				monUse+="-"+$(this).val();
			}}
		)
		location.href="http://www1.10086.cn/apps/feePack/search.do?provId="+451+"&brand="+brand+"&busiTrend="+busiTrend+"&monUse="+monUse+"&cityId="+1000451;
	}

<script type="text/javascript">
	//显示省
	$("#showProv").mouseover(function(){$("#feeDivProv").show()});
	$("#showProv").mouseout(function(){$("#feeDivProv").hide()});
	 if("黑龙江"=="北京" || "黑龙江"=="上海" || "黑龙江"=="海南" || "黑龙江"=="重庆" || "黑龙江"=="天津"){
     $('#showCity').css('display','none');
    }
	//计算总页数
	function countFullPages(maxentries,look){
		if(look=="list"){
			return Math.ceil(maxentries/6);
		}else if(look=="big"){
			return Math.ceil(maxentries/9);
		}else{
			return 0;
		}
	}
	now_page = 0;
	leftBind=0;
	rightBind=1;
	$("#arrowLeft").bind("click",function(){pagination(current_brand,current_type,current_look,current_order,--now_page)}).removeClass().addClass("page_btn_l");

	$("#arrowRight").bind("click",function(){pagination(current_brand,current_type,current_look,current_order,++now_page)}).removeClass().addClass("page_btn_r");
		//开始分页
	function pagination(brand,type,look,order,page){
		var max_elem = 0;
		var items_per_page = 0;
		var maxentries = getFullNumsAndPages(brand,type,look)[0];
		var item_class = "feeItem_big";
		
		if(look=="list"&&maxentries>0){
			items_per_page = 6;
			$("#look_list").removeClass().addClass("list_show_btn_l");
			$("#look_big").removeClass().addClass("list_show_btn_r_false");
			item_class = "feeItem_list";
			max_elem = Math.min((now_page*1+1) * items_per_page,maxentries);
		}
		if(look=="big"&&maxentries>0){
			items_per_page = 9;

			$("#look_list").removeClass().addClass("list_show_btn_l_false");
			$("#look_big").removeClass().addClass("list_show_btn_r");
			item_class = "feeItem_big";
			max_elem = Math.min((now_page*1+1) * items_per_page,maxentries);
		}
		
		$(".fee_tab_box2").html("");
		//显示套餐总数
		$("#fee_num").html(maxentries);
		
		// 获取加载元素
		for(var i=now_page*items_per_page;i<max_elem;i++){
		$(".fee_tab_box2").append($("#"+brand+"_"+type+"_"+look+"_"+order+"_hidden ."+item_class+":eq("+i+")").clone());
		}
		//页面上方分页
		var pageNums = countFullPages(maxentries,look);
		$(".page_no").html("").append("<span class='cheng'>"+(now_page*1+1)+"</span>/"+pageNums);
		//页面下方分页
		$(".page_1").html("").append("共"+(now_page*1+1)+"/"+pageNums+"页&nbsp;&nbsp;每页"+items_per_page+"项&nbsp;&nbsp;共"+maxentries+"项");
		
		//默认option
		var cur_max_page_nums = getFullNumsAndPages(brand,type,look)[1];
		/*原下拉框
		$("#jumpMenu").html("");
		for(var j=0;j<cur_max_page_nums;j++){
			$("#jumpMenu").append("<option value='"+j+"'>"+(j+1)+"</option>");
		}
		$("#jumpMenu").val(now_page);*/
		
		//页码到底改变箭头样式
		if(now_page<=0){
			$("#arrowLeft").unbind("click").removeClass().addClass("page_btn_l_false");
			leftBind=0;
			if(now_page>=cur_max_page_nums-1){
				$("#arrowRight").unbind("click").removeClass().addClass("page_btn_r_false");
				rightBind=0;
			}else{
				if(rightBind==0){
				$("#arrowRight").bind("click",function(){pagination(brand,type,look,order,++now_page)}).removeClass().addClass("page_btn_r");
			    rightBind++;
			    }else{
			    $("#arrowRight").unbind("click");
			    $("#arrowRight").bind("click",function(){pagination(brand,type,look,order,++now_page)});
			    }
			}
		}else if(now_page>0&&now_page<cur_max_page_nums-1){
			if(leftBind==0){
			$("#arrowLeft").bind("click",function(){pagination(brand,type,look,order,--now_page)}).removeClass().addClass("page_btn_l");
			leftBind++;
			}else{
			$("#arrowLeft").unbind("click");
			$("#arrowLeft").bind("click",function(){pagination(brand,type,look,order,--now_page)});
			}
            if(rightBind==0){          
			$("#arrowRight").bind("click",function(){pagination(brand,type,look,order,++now_page)}).removeClass().addClass("page_btn_r");
            rightBind++;
            }else{
             $("#arrowRight").unbind("click");
             $("#arrowRight").bind("click",function(){pagination(brand,type,look,order,++now_page)});
            }
		}else{
			$("#arrowRight").unbind("click").removeClass().addClass("page_btn_r_false");
			rightBind=0;
			if(leftBind==0){
			$("#arrowLeft").bind("click",function(){pagination(brand,type,look,order,--now_page)}).removeClass().addClass("page_btn_l");
			leftBind++;
			}else{
			$("#arrowLeft").unbind("click");
			$("#arrowLeft").bind("click",function(){pagination(brand,type,look,order,--now_page)});
			}
		}
		
	}

	//获取对应总套餐数及总页数
	function getFullNumsAndPages(brand,type,look){
		if(brand=="gotone"){
			if(type=="call"){
				if(look=="list"){
					return [gotone_call_num,gotone_call_list_pages];
				}else{
					return [gotone_call_num,gotone_call_big_pages];
				}	
			}else if(type=="flow"){
				if(look=="list"){
					return [gotone_flow_num,gotone_flow_list_pages];
				}else{
					return [gotone_flow_num,gotone_flow_big_pages];
				}
			}else{
				if(look=="list"){
					return [gotone_data_num,gotone_data_list_pages];
				}else{
					return [gotone_data_num,gotone_data_big_pages];
				}
			}
		}else if(brand=="mzone"){
			if(type=="call"){
				if(look=="list"){
					return [mzone_call_num,mzone_call_list_pages];
				}else{
					return [mzone_call_num,mzone_call_big_pages];
				}	
			}else if(type=="flow"){
				if(look=="list"){
					return [mzone_flow_num,mzone_flow_list_pages];
				}else{
					return [mzone_flow_num,mzone_flow_big_pages];
				}
			}else{
				if(look=="list"){
					return [mzone_data_num,mzone_data_list_pages];
				}else{
					return [mzone_data_num,mzone_data_big_pages];
				}
			}
		}else{
			if(type=="call"){
				if(look=="list"){
					return [easyown_call_num,easyown_call_list_pages];
				}else{
					return [easyown_call_num,easyown_call_big_pages];
				}	
			}else if(type=="flow"){
				if(look=="list"){
					return [easyown_flow_num,easyown_flow_list_pages];
				}else{
					return [easyown_flow_num,easyown_flow_big_pages];
				}
			}else{
				if(look=="list"){
					return [easyown_data_num,easyown_data_list_pages];
				}else{
					return [easyown_data_num,easyown_data_big_pages];
				}
			}
		}
	}

		window.open("http://www.10086.cn/4G/");
	})

	})

	$("div.fee_fl span:eq(0)").bind("click",function(){
		current_type = 'call';now_page = 0;pagination(current_brand,current_type,current_look,current_order,current_page);
		checkOrderStatus(current_brand,current_type,current_click_order);
		$(this).removeClass().addClass("fee_fl_btn_active").siblings().removeClass().addClass("fee_fl_btn");
		$("div.txt:eq(0) span").html("话音套餐");
	})
	$("div.fee_fl span:eq(1)").bind("click",function(){
		current_type = 'flow';now_page = 0;pagination(current_brand,current_type,current_look,current_order,current_page);
		checkOrderStatus(current_brand,current_type,current_click_order);
		$(this).removeClass().addClass("fee_fl_btn_active").siblings().removeClass().addClass("fee_fl_btn");

	})

	$("#look_list").bind("click",function(){
	    now_page=0;
		current_look = 'list';pagination(current_brand,current_type,current_look,current_order,current_page);

	})

	now_page=0;

		$(this).removeClass().addClass("list_show_btn_r").siblings().removeClass().addClass("list_show_btn_l_false");
	})
	
	var left_window = 0;
	var top_window = 0;
	//省会添加弹框应用
	if("哈尔滨"=="合肥"||"哈尔滨"=="福州"||"哈尔滨"=="广州"||"哈尔滨"=="兰州"||"哈尔滨"=="南宁"||"哈尔滨"=="贵阳"||"哈尔滨"=="郑州"||"哈尔滨"=="武汉"||"哈尔滨"=="石家庄"||"哈尔滨"=="哈尔滨"||"哈尔滨"=="长沙"||"哈尔滨"=="长春"||"哈尔滨"=="南京"||"哈尔滨"=="南昌"||"哈尔滨"=="沈阳"||"哈尔滨"=="呼和浩特"||"哈尔滨"=="银川"||"哈尔滨"=="西宁"||"哈尔滨"=="成都"||"哈尔滨"=="济南"||"哈尔滨"=="西安"||"哈尔滨"=="太原"||"哈尔滨"=="乌鲁木齐"||"哈尔滨"=="拉萨"||"哈尔滨"=="昆明"||"哈尔滨"=="杭州"){
		
		$("<div/>").attr("id","windowWrap").css({"display":"none","width":"100%","height":"100%","position":"fixed","top":"0","left":"0","opacity":"0.5","filter":"alpha(opacity=50)","background":"#222","z-index":"999998"}).appendTo($("body"));
		$(".closeBtn").bind("click",function(){$('.feeJumpWindow').hide();$('#windowWrap').hide();});
		
		//$(".feeJumpWindow ul a").bind("click",function(){writeFeeCookie});
		
		function showPop(){
			$('.feeJumpWindow').css({
				position:'absolute',
				"z-index":'999999',
				left: ($(window).width() - $('.feeJumpWindow').outerWidth())/2,
				top: ($(window).height() - $('.feeJumpWindow').outerHeight())/2 + $(document).scrollTop()
			});
			$('#windowWrap').show();
			$('.feeJumpWindow').show();
			left_window = $(".feeJumpWindow").offset().left;
			top_window = $(".feeJumpWindow").offset().top;
		}

		$(window).scroll(function() {
			var top = $(window).scrollTop(); 
			var left= $(window).scrollLeft();
			$(".feeJumpWindow").css({ left:left+left_window+ "px", top: top+top_window+ "px" }); 
		});
		
		//var zf_city_code;
		if(document.cookie.indexOf("CmCitycode")==-1){
			$(window).resize(function(){showPop()});
			//初始化函数
			$(window).resize();
		}	
	}	
</script>
</body>
</html>
